namespace = randomeventsstapehordes
country_event = {
	id = randomeventsstapehordes.1
	title = "randomeventsstapehordes.1.EVTNAME"
	desc = "randomeventsstapehordes.1.EVTDESC"
	picture = HORDE_ON_HORSEBACK_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_reform = steppe_horde
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = title_6
						has_country_flag = title_6
					}
				}
				has_reform = steppe_horde_legacy
			}
		}
		is_at_war = no
		NOT = {
			had_recent_war = 2
		}
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				superregion = central_asia_superregion
				superregion = eastern_steppe_superregion
				region = crimea_region
				region = steppes_region
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			NOT = {
				MIL = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "randomeventsstapehordes.1.EVTOPTA"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_prestige = -5
	}
	option = {
		name = "randomeventsstapehordes.1.EVTOPTB"
		trigger = {
			has_idea_group = administrative_ideas
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				prestige = 50
			}
		}
		add_army_tradition = -5
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = randomeventsstapehordes.19
	title = "randomeventsstapehordes.19.EVTNAME"
	desc = "randomeventsstapehordes.19.EVTDESC"
	picture = HORDE_ON_HORSEBACK_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_tribal = yes
			is_nomad = yes
		}
		has_heir = yes
		heir_age = 11
		has_female_heir = no
		AND = {
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
				is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
			}
		}
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = {
			legitimacy_or_horde_unity = 50
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = "randomeventsstapehordes.19.EVTOPTA"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_prestige = -2
		random_list = {
			30 = {}
			50 = {
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_lost_50
				hidden_effect = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = stability_points
									value = 0
								}
							}
						}
						add_stability = -1
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.003
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_emperor_of_china = yes
							}
							add_mandate = -5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				add_stability = -1
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.003
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -5
				}
			}
		}
		kill_heir = yes
	}
}

									value = 0

		random_list = {
